LAW DEPARTMENT
LIST OF NOTARIES APPOINTED AND IN PRACTICE AT THE BEGINNING OF THE YEAR 2022
(See rule 17)
[G.O. Ms. No. 33, Law (Administration), 29th January 2022, Thai 16, Pilava, Thiruvalluvar Aandu-2053.]
No.II(2)/LAW/70(dd)/2022
In exercise of the powers conferred by Section 6 of the Notaries Act, 1952 (Central Act LIII of 1952), Governor of 
Tamil Nadu hereby publishes the following list of Notaries appointed by the Government of Tamil Nadu and practice at the 
beginning of the year 2022.
